I've heard that there's not many natural ingredients in perfumery, so to make a fragrance smell natural is quite hard to do. Chanel and Louis Vuitton certainly do a good job at bringing good perfumery, balance and quality into their fragrances of course with a few exceptions like imagination and meteore smelling rather cheap. Symphony however doesn't smell cheap and manages to capture the high quality smell, also for the price yes it's expensive but it also smells expensive you will immediately know it's an expensive fragrance when you smell it just by how good the quality it. I struggle to find many good quality brands and fragrances Armani does make pretty good quality fragrances too though but like acqua di gio flankers everyone seems to be wearing them and makes them off putting to by if everyone wears the same thing. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2322997" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="santeripe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1350593"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1350593.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="santeripe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rania-J/Musc-Moschus-54877.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.54877.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Musc Moschus"title="Musc Moschus"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2322997ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2322997" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1350593">santeripe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-21">10/21/24 12:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On paper this smells exactly like a Glade bathroom air freshener. The ozonic ingredients pop out heavily. On skin the opening/mid is quite beautiful with elegance and class to it. However, after an hour or two the scent gets rougher and rougher around the edges. It stays smelling citrus, just more and more synthetic. Ultimately veering into that ozonic air freshener territory.<br />
<br />
This fragrance lasts for hours as a citrus is because there's very little actual citrus here. The scent of grapefruit has been recreated using long-lasting molecules like floralozone, ambroxan, aldehydes, calone, fruity musks etc. I think this being marketed with 3 notes is fair, as that's what the perfumer tried to convey. The musks and ambroxan here aren't presented as themselves. They're trying their best to not be noticed, playing together to mimic citrus.<br />
<br />
It is an interesting concept in perfumery to synthetically recreate a citrus top note using base notes! And that is something this fragrance does better than anything else I've tried. The different aspects of citrus, like juiciness, brightness, freshness and oiliness of the peel have been recreated using various long-lasting base ingredients. But there's a reason why it's not done more often. No matter how well and expertly the scent is blended, you can ultimately always tell that it's a blend of synthetics. Especially after the mid notes wear off. It's a no from me for this massive price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68357"comment_id="2322997"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Symphony-68357.html?ccid=2322997#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305075" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A bergamot and grapefruit done very well. This scent doesn't have much to it, but it definitely doesn't need it, the simplicity somehow stands out to me, how it's just light, blissful, and as the name suggests, symphony.<br />
<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
It's has light to moderate projection, but I feel like it wouldn't be good if it was strong, the lightness contributes to the vibe of this fragrance.<br />
<br />
Longevity: 6/10<br />
Just a regular 5-6 hours, nothing special.<br />
<br />
Is it worth the price (320USD): 4/10<br />
Probably not, this price is pretty outrageous, however, you might like it, give it a try and see if you like it/<br />
<br />
Final Rating: 7.7 / 10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68357"comment_id="2254346"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Symphony-68357.html?ccid=2254346#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2240711" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; She greeted me, and my initial reaction was, "What the heck are you wearing? That smells so good." She then reiterated that it was the fragrance from your car! I was like, "What? Are you kidding me?" She said no and mentioned that people had been asking her what she was wearing all day. <br />
<br />
I went ahead and ordered the bottle right before Christmas; by then, I was traveling. The morning before going to the airport, I applied 10-12 sprays all over. When I got to the airport, a security lady stopped me and asked the name of the fragrance I was wearing. Moving along, I got to the Capital One Venture X lounge. While seated and having a drink, a young lady passing by stopped. She was one of the servers. Her exact words were, "Oh, it's you we've been smelling. You smell really amazing. What is it that you're wearing?" <br />
<br />
I've had similar experiences with "Imagination" and other fragrances, but this one takes the cake by far. I see people bashing this fragrance, but until you have smelled it second-hand, you will never see the beauty of it. I had the sample my car for months and thought it gave me Aventus vibes, but I was wrong. <br />
If this is the only LV fragrance you buy/have AND you‚Äôre able to get it at a price that is more reasonable, then it offers a good path into the LV ‚Äúfresh‚Äù profile.  Of the 8-9 LV fragrances I own or have tried (usual suspects‚Ä¶ Imagination, L‚ÄôImmensite, Meteore, Pacific Chill, Afternoon Swim, Sur le Route, Orage, On the Beach, Symphony) they are all far more similar than different (I‚Äôd say 80%, some of them 90% similar).  In my opinion, all of them will invoke familiar scent profiles that you‚Äôd find in $80-$100 designer fragrances, but several provide a step up in ingredient quality and, in some cases, depth that you won‚Äôt find in most (all?) designer fragrances.  To my nose, Symphony doesn‚Äôt after anything meaningfully incremental to justify the extra price, though perhaps slightly longer performance than a couple of the shortest lasting.<br />
<br />
Of the ones I‚Äôve owned/tried, I prefer the following over this (in no particular order)  (1) Afternoon Swim - which smells similar to Creed MI, but done even better IMO (2) L‚ÄôImmensite which has quality nuance and depth that makes it stand above the designer tiers (3) On the beach - which has a nice / unique white floral background while still being masculine enough to wear and still invoking a beach vacation (4) Pacific Chill which offers a really nice , but subtle fruit and mint blend (5) Imagination - which settles down into the smell of a yellow Dial soap bar, but in a way / quality that still makes keep coming back to it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
I love citrus scents, and this is no exception. However, Symphony goes extremely flat- like a body spray and literally makes you question "what note is this missing??..." The ginger is definitely there, but it's lacking that spicy sweet "zing" of fresh ginger...YET Symphony is so clean and fresh, like a high end citrus scent should be. It is photorealistic, like you just sliced a ripe grapefruit and were sprayed with the zest of the peel. <br />
<br />
If money is no object, this would make perfect sense for a citrus lover. I can also think of a million layering combos with this as well that would make me smell like I just walked off a mega yacht in Antibes on a nice summer day... I had no problem throwing my coins at Roses Les Sables and Ombre Nomad however, at $560.00 Symphony is just so hard to justify. At the end of the day I would love to get my hands on a full bottle, but no way near the retail price... but just as a toxic relationship goes, I may be running back to buy this no expense spared...</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Underselling the fragrance IMO.<br />
<br />
Imagine someone had selected the sweetest possible variants of a bunch of citrus fruits. Grapefruit, mandarin, orange, lemon, pomelo and bergamot. Sparkly, juicy, zingy, effervescent, natural, uplifting, fresh, energizing, sweet and clean. A slight hint of something aquatic and ozonic gives it a slightly watery aspect that blends very delicately with the hint of white florals and the sheer, transparent musk. <br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1925038" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ground hound"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1589008"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1589008.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ground hound" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Olfactive-Studio/Iris-Shot-54869.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.54869.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Iris Shot"title="Iris Shot"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1925038ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1925038" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1589008">Ground hound</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-11">09/11/23 03:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A Very Sweet floral citrus with strawberry and a complex ending.<br />
Starts off very warm, unlike many cold citrus scents nowadays.<br />
It starts as a candied yet juicy grapefruit, flows into strawberry-apricot-powder-floral feminine mix and ends as a bit artificial (don`t want to say cheap) lemon. I don`t mind it but I can see how this can be a turn-off.<br />
Can`t smell any ginger or bergamot, I think there are lots of other notes missing from the description.<br />
Basically if you spray yourself with a powdery strawberry-apricot scent and go boil a grapefruit in a pot with sugar syrup- this is going to be the smell.<br />
Overpriced, but I did like it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68357"comment_id="1925038"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Symphony-68357.html?ccid=1925038#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1924094" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1236771">Vannamae__</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-03">04/03/23 10:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I‚Äôm writing another review on this because I got a FB months ago, been wearing it a lot and I‚Äôm happy to report my initial feelings are still the same. The performance for a fresh scent is amazing. I wear this to the gym to workout a lot and even after 1 1/2 hours of lifting and another 30 mins of cardio it was still going strong. I could smell it as I moved and it does get a lot of compliments. Probably because it‚Äôs mass appealing and hard to not notice as it just radiates off of you. On a breezy day, the scent smells so good on a walk. On a non workout day when I‚Äôm not sweating my ass off, this scent lasts 8-10 hours and projects for a good 6 before getting closer to the skin. <br />
<br />
Yes it is still a bit overpriced because of the brand name and I still think the cap would have looked better in the regular style but this fragrance is a powerhouse for a freshie and that is pretty rare. It is so uplifting, very linear but I enjoy that about it. I own a lot of complex scents and this is a great break from those. While it is linear, I still find it unique and it is an absolute joy to wear. I tried a few others in this particular line but this was the stand out in scent and performance wise. Perfect fragrance for spring and hot summer days.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68357"comment_id="1799423"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Symphony-68357.html?ccid=1799423#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1775994" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It continued hitting me for several hours until eventually it got tired of it and curled up on my skin.  It did lose its bitterness (finally!) and dried down into something that resembles pleasant. <br />

I also liked Rhapsody and Cosmic Cloud. <br />
Symphony is my favorite because it's universal: it smells classy, pleasant, inoffensive and it's unisex. It can be worn to the office and to an event or when going out. I'd describe it as deep, complex, citrus scent. It's well blended and not harsh.<br />
It's a luxury category for the price point so there's a small chance you will smell like everyone else.<br />
The bottle and the cap has interesting design that is pleasant to look at.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68357"comment_id="1661272"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Symphony-68357.html?ccid=1661272#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="68357" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
